The given statement "You start quarrels with others" does not align well with the description of being low in Emotional Stability (high in Neuroticism), low in Agreeableness, and high in Openness to Experience. People who are high in Openness to Experience often have an expansive view of the world and may engage more in creative or philosophical pursuits rather than starting conflicts. However, the statement could be seen as potentially accurate if we consider the possibility that someone high in Openness might also have strong opinions or a tendency to challenge norms or beliefs, which could sometimes lead to conflict. Given the specific traits provided, it leans towards being inaccurate.
